(**********************************************************************************************

 First-order Hyperdoctrines

 Hyperdoctrines provide a framework in which one can interpret the basic judgments of
 first-order predicate logic. However, if one actually wants to study predicate logic, then
 one also needs to have suitable connectives for the formulas, and one also needs to have an
 equality predicate.

 In this file, we define first-order hyperdoctrines. First-order hyperdoctrines are an extension
 of ordinary hyperdoctrines. In a first-order hyperdoctrine, we can interpret all the usual
 connectives from first-order predicate logic and equality. Note that we focus on intuitionistic
 first-order hyperdoctrines, so the law of excluded middle does not hold in them. For each of
 the connectives, we also define accessors, which are similar to the elimination and introduction
 rules in natural deduction.

 Note that the connectives are defined as follows:
 - Truth: fiberwise terminal object
 - Falsity: fiberwise initial object
 - Conjunction: fiberwise binary products
 - Disjunction: fiberwise binary coproducts
 - Implication: fiberwise exponentials
 - Universal quantification: right adjoint to substitution
 - Existential quantification: left adjoint to substitution
 - Equality: left adjoint to the diagonal
 For the propositional connectives, the introduction and elimination rules arise rather directly
 from the definition of limits and colimits, whereas their preservation under substitution
 follow from the fiberwise preservation. For the quantifiers, their preservation under
 substitution follows from the Beck-Chevalley condition, and their introduction and elimination
 rules follow from the unit and counit of the adjunctions.

 Technically there are some interesting points in this file. To derive the elimination rule for
 disjunction, we use distributivity of products and coproducts. This follows from the fact that
 we have exponentials. As such, taking the binary product with a fixed object is a left adjoint,
 and it thus preserves coproducts.

 Another point arises from the existential quantification. The elimination rule for the
 existential quantifier says that `Δ ⊢ ψ` follows from `Δ ⊢ ∃ φ` and `Δ ∧ φ ⊢ ψ`. To derive this
 rule, we need Frobenius reciprocity, which says that `∃ (Δ ∧ φ)` follows from `Δ ∧ ∃ φ`. Without
 this assumption, we would only be able to derive a weaker rule, where we need to show `φ ⊢ ψ`,
 so without the assumptions in `Δ`. To prove Frobenius reciprocity, we use the implication.

 The equality formula also comes with an introduction and elimination rule. From the elimination
 rule, we can derive symmetry and transitivity of equality. The proof is similar to how one uses
 the J-rule to derive symmetry and transitivity of the identity type. We also derive equality
 principles for terms of the unit type and of the product type. To prove the desired J-rule, we
 use that our hyperdoctrines support universal quantification.

 Finally, note that in our definition, we require left and right adjoints to exist for
 substitution along all morphisms rather than just projections. This is stronger than one would
 usually require, and it does eliminate the syntax as a model. However, in many models all
 of the aforementioned adjoints do exist.

 An important use case of first-order hyperdoctrines is using the internal language for reasoning.
 The internal language is implemented via a shallow embedding. However, one challenge that one
 meets when using this shallow embedding directly, is that one must simplify the goal completely
 by hand. More concretely, there might be several substitutions in the statement that one is
 proving, and to simplify it, one must rewrite using the right substitution laws. The same holds
 for normalizing terms: one must simplify every β-redex by using an appropriate rewrite statement.
 In this file, we also give a tactic that automates these processes. Below we comment on the
 design of this tactic and in the file `PERs.v` in the proof of [eq_per_axioms], we explain
 and demonstrate how this tactic is used.

 References
 - "Adjointness in Foundations" by William Lawvere
 - "Categorical logic" by Andrew Pitts in Handbook of logic in computer science, Volume 5
 - "Tripos Theory in Retrospect" by Andrew Pitts

 Content
 1. First-order hyperdoctrines
 2. The truth formula
 3. The falsity formula
 4. Conjunction
 5. Weakening of hypotheses
 6. Disjunction
 7. Implication
 8. Universal quantification
 9. Existential quantification
 10. Equality
 11. Derived rules for equality
 12. Derived connectives
 12.1. Bi-implication
 13. A tactic for simplifying goals in the internal language of first-order hyperdoctrines

 **********************************************************************************************)

(** * 1. First-order hyperdoctrines *)
Definition first_order_preorder_hyperdoctrine
  : UU
  := ∑ (H : preorder_hyperdoctrine),
     fiberwise_terminal (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)
     ×
     fiberwise_initial (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)
     ×
     ∑ (P : fiberwise_binproducts (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)),
     fiberwise_bincoproducts (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)
     ×
     fiberwise_exponentials P
     ×
     has_dependent_products (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)
     ×
     has_dependent_sums (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H).


H: first_order_preorder_hyperdoctrine
preorder_hyperdoctrine


H: first_order_preorder_hyperdoctrine
preorder_hyperdoctrine

  exact (pr1 H).
Defined.

Definition first_order_hyperdoctrine
  : UU
  := ∑ (H : hyperdoctrine),
     fiberwise_terminal (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)
     ×
     fiberwise_initial (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)
     ×
     ∑ (P : fiberwise_binproducts (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)),
     fiberwise_bincoproducts (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)
     ×
     fiberwise_exponentials P
     ×
     has_dependent_products (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)
     ×
     has_dependent_sums (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H).


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
hyperdoctrine


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
hyperdoctrine

  exact (pr1 H).
Defined.


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
first_order_preorder_hyperdoctrine


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
first_order_preorder_hyperdoctrine

  exact (_
         ,,
         pr12 H
         ,,
         pr122 H
         ,,
         pr1 (pr222 H)
         ,,
         pr12 (pr222 H)
         ,,
         pr122 (pr222 H)
         ,,
         pr1 (pr222 (pr222 H))
         ,,
         pr2 (pr222 (pr222 H))).
Defined.

Definition univalent_first_order_hyperdoctrine
  : UU
  := ∑ (H : univalent_hyperdoctrine),
     fiberwise_terminal (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)
     ×
     fiberwise_initial (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)
     ×
     ∑ (P : fiberwise_binproducts (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)),
     fiberwise_bincoproducts (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)
     ×
     fiberwise_exponentials P
     ×
     has_dependent_products (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H)
     ×
     has_dependent_sums (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H).


H: univalent_first_order_hyperdoctrine
univalent_hyperdoctrine


H: univalent_first_order_hyperdoctrine

  exact (pr1 H).
Defined.


H: univalent_first_order_hyperdoctrine
first_order_hyperdoctrine


H: univalent_first_order_hyperdoctrine
first_order_hyperdoctrine

  exact (_
         ,,
         pr12 H
         ,,
         pr122 H
         ,,
         pr1 (pr222 H)
         ,,
         pr12 (pr222 H)
         ,,
         pr122 (pr222 H)
         ,,
         pr1 (pr222 (pr222 H))
         ,,
         pr2 (pr222 (pr222 H))).
Defined.

Definition make_first_order_preorder_hyperdoctrine
           (H : preorder_hyperdoctrine)
           (TH : fiberwise_terminal (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (IH : fiberwise_initial (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (PH : fiberwise_binproducts (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (CH : fiberwise_bincoproducts (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (IMPH : fiberwise_exponentials PH)
           (DPH : has_dependent_products (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (DSH : has_dependent_sums (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
  : first_order_preorder_hyperdoctrine
  := H
     ,,
     TH
     ,,
     IH
     ,,
     PH
     ,,
     CH
     ,,
     IMPH
     ,,
     DPH
     ,,
     DSH.

Definition make_first_order_hyperdoctrine
           (H : hyperdoctrine)
           (TH : fiberwise_terminal (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (IH : fiberwise_initial (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (PH : fiberwise_binproducts (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (CH : fiberwise_bincoproducts (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (IMPH : fiberwise_exponentials PH)
           (DPH : has_dependent_products (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (DSH : has_dependent_sums (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
  : first_order_hyperdoctrine
  := H
     ,,
     TH
     ,,
     IH
     ,,
     PH
     ,,
     CH
     ,,
     IMPH
     ,,
     DPH
     ,,
     DSH.

Definition make_univalent_first_order_hyperdoctrine
           (H : univalent_hyperdoctrine)
           (TH : fiberwise_terminal (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (IH : fiberwise_initial (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (PH : fiberwise_binproducts (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (CH : fiberwise_bincoproducts (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (IMPH : fiberwise_exponentials PH)
           (DPH : has_dependent_products (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
           (DSH : has_dependent_sums (hyperdoctrine_cleaving H))
  : univalent_first_order_hyperdoctrine
  := H
     ,,
     TH
     ,,
     IH
     ,,
     PH
     ,,
     CH
     ,,
     IMPH
     ,,
     DPH
     ,,
     DSH.

(** * 2. The truth formula *)
Definition first_order_hyperdoctrine_truth
           {H : first_order_hyperdoctrine}
           {Γ : ty H}
  : form Γ
  := terminal_obj_in_fib (pr12 H) Γ.

Notation "'⊤'" := first_order_hyperdoctrine_truth : hyperdoctrine.


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ: form Γ
Δ ⊢ ⊤


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ: form Γ
Δ ⊢ ⊤

  exact (TerminalArrow (terminal_in_fib (pr12 H) Γ) Δ).
Qed.


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂: ty H
s: tm Γ₁ Γ₂
⊤ [s] = ⊤


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂: ty H
s: tm Γ₁ Γ₂
⊤ [s] = ⊤

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂: ty H
s: tm Γ₁ Γ₂
is_univalent_disp (hyperdoctrine_formula_disp_cat H)
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂: ty H
s: tm Γ₁ Γ₂
z_iso_disp (idtoiso (idpath Γ₁))
  (pr1 ((pr122 (pr22 H)) Γ₂ Γ₁ s ⊤)) ⊤

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂: ty H
s: tm Γ₁ Γ₂
is_univalent_disp (hyperdoctrine_formula_disp_cat H)
 apply is_univalent_disp_hyperdoctrine.
  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂: ty H
s: tm Γ₁ Γ₂
z_iso_disp (idtoiso (idpath Γ₁))
  (pr1 ((pr122 (pr22 H)) Γ₂ Γ₁ s ⊤)) ⊤
 
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂: ty H
s: tm Γ₁ Γ₂
z_iso (pr1 ((pr122 (pr22 H)) Γ₂ Γ₁ s ⊤)) ⊤

    apply (preserves_terminal_to_z_iso _ (pr212 H _ _ s) _ _).
Qed.

(** * 3. The falsity formula *)
Definition first_order_hyperdoctrine_false
           {H : first_order_hyperdoctrine}
           {Γ : ty H}
  : form Γ
  := initial_obj_in_fib (pr122 H) Γ.

Notation "'⊥'" := first_order_hyperdoctrine_false : hyperdoctrine.

⊥ ⊢ φ

  exact (InitialArrow (initial_in_fib (pr122 H) Γ) φ).
Qed.

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂: ty H

(** * 4. Conjunction *)
Definition first_order_hyperdoctrine_conj
           {H : first_order_hyperdoctrine}
           {Γ : ty H}
           (φ ψ : form Γ)
  : form Γ
  := BinProductObject _ (binprod_in_fib (pr1 (pr222 H)) φ ψ).

Notation "φ ∧ ψ" := (first_order_hyperdoctrine_conj φ ψ).


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ φ
q: Δ ⊢ ψ
Δ ⊢ φ ∧ ψ


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ φ
q: Δ ⊢ ψ
Δ ⊢ φ ∧ ψ

  exact (BinProductArrow _ (binprod_in_fib (pr1 (pr222 H)) φ ψ) p q).
Qed.


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ φ ∧ ψ
Δ ⊢ φ


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ φ ∧ ψ
Δ ⊢ φ

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ φ ∧ ψ
φ ∧ ψ ⊢ φ

  apply (BinProductPr1 _ (binprod_in_fib (pr1 (pr222 H)) φ ψ)).
Qed.


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ φ ∧ ψ
Δ ⊢ ψ


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H

φ ∧ ψ ⊢ ψ

  apply (BinProductPr2 _ (binprod_in_fib (pr1 (pr222 H)) φ ψ)).
Qed.

φ, ψ: form Γ₂
z_iso (pr1 ((pr122 (pr22 H)) Γ₂ Γ₁ s (φ ∧ ψ)))
  (φ [s] ∧ ψ [s])

    use (preserves_binproduct_to_z_iso _ (pr21 (pr222 H) _ _ s)).
Qed.

(** * 5. Weakening of hypotheses *)

(**
   The presence of conjunction allows us to add assumptions to the formula context.
   We can derive the proper weaking rules for that.
 *)

Δ₁ ∧ Δ₂ ⊢ φ

(** * 6. Disjunction *)
Definition first_order_hyperdoctrine_disj
           {H : first_order_hyperdoctrine}
           {Γ : ty H}
           (φ ψ : form Γ)
  : form Γ
  := BinCoproductObject (bincoprod_in_fib (pr12 (pr222 H)) φ ψ).

Notation "φ ∨ ψ" := (first_order_hyperdoctrine_disj φ ψ).


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ φ
Δ ⊢ φ ∨ ψ


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ φ
Δ ⊢ φ ∨ ψ

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ φ
φ ⊢ φ ∨ ψ

  apply (BinCoproductIn1 (bincoprod_in_fib (pr12 (pr222 H)) φ ψ)).
Qed.


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ ψ
Δ ⊢ φ ∨ ψ


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ ψ
Δ ⊢ φ ∨ ψ

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ ψ
ψ ⊢ φ ∨ ψ

  apply (BinCoproductIn2 (bincoprod_in_fib (pr12 (pr222 H)) φ ψ)).
Qed.


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
φ, ψ, χ: form Γ
φ ∧ (ψ ∨ χ) ⊢ φ ∧ ψ ∨ φ ∧ χ


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
φ, ψ, χ: form Γ
φ ∧ (ψ ∨ χ) ⊢ φ ∧ ψ ∨ φ ∧ χ

  exact (pr1 (distributivity_fiberwise_exponentials
                (pr12 (pr222 H))
                (pr122 (pr222 H))
                φ ψ χ)).
Defined.


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ, χ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ φ ∨ ψ
q: Δ ∧ φ ⊢ χ
r: Δ ∧ ψ ⊢ χ
Δ ⊢ χ


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ, χ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ φ ∨ ψ
q: Δ ∧ φ ⊢ χ
r: Δ ∧ ψ ⊢ χ
Δ ⊢ χ

p: Δ ⊢ φ ∨ ψ
q: Δ ∧ φ ⊢ χ
r: Δ ∧ ψ ⊢ χ
Δ ⊢ bincoprod_in_fib (pr122 (pr22 H)) (Δ ∧ φ) (Δ ∧ ψ)

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ: ty H
Δ, φ, ψ, χ: form Γ
p: Δ ⊢ φ ∨ ψ
q: Δ ∧ φ ⊢ χ
r: Δ ∧ ψ ⊢ χ
Δ ∧ (φ ∨ ψ)
⊢ bincoprod_in_fib (pr122 (pr22 H)) (Δ ∧ φ) (Δ ∧ ψ)

  apply distributivity.
Qed.

  (pr1 ((pr122 (pr22 H)) Γ₂ Γ₁ s (φ ∨ ψ)))
  (φ [s] ∨ ψ [s])

Qed.

(** * 8. Universal quantification *)
Definition first_order_hyperdoctrine_forall
           {H : first_order_hyperdoctrine}
           {Γ A : ty H}
           (φ : form (Γ ×h A))
  : form Γ
  := dep_prod (pr1 (pr222 (pr222 H))) (π₁ (identity (Γ ×h A))) φ.

Notation "'∀h' φ" := (first_order_hyperdoctrine_forall φ) (at level 10)
    : hyperdoctrine.


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ⊢ φ
Δ ⊢ ∀h φ


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ⊢ φ
Δ ⊢ ∀h φ

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ⊢ φ
dep_prod (pr122 (pr222 (pr2 H)))
  (π₁ (identity (Γ ×h A)))
  (fiber_functor_from_cleaving (pr12 (pr1 H))
     (hyperdoctrine_cleaving (pr1 H))
     (π₁ (identity (Γ ×h A))) Δ) ⊢ ∀h φ

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ⊢ φ
(pr12 (pr1 H))[{Γ ×h A}]
⟦ fiber_functor_from_cleaving (pr12 (pr1 H))
    (hyperdoctrine_cleaving (pr1 H))
    (π₁ (identity (Γ ×h A))) Δ, φ ⟧

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ⊢ φ
(pr122 (pr221 H)) Γ (Γ ×h A) (π₁ (identity (Γ ×h A)))
  Δ -->[ identity (Γ ×h A)] φ

  exact p.
Qed.


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ ⊢ ∀h φ
t: tm Γ A
Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ ⊢ ∀h φ
t: tm Γ A
Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ ⊢ ∀h φ
t: tm Γ A
∀h φ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ ⊢ ∀h φ
t: tm Γ A
(∀h φ) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ⊢ φ
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ ⊢ ∀h φ
t: tm Γ A
r: (∀h φ) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ⊢ φ
∀h φ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ ⊢ ∀h φ
t: tm Γ A
(∀h φ) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ⊢ φ

    exact (dep_prod_counit (pr1 (pr222 (pr222 H))) (π₁ (identity (Γ ×h A))) φ).
  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ ⊢ ∀h φ
t: tm Γ A
r: (∀h φ) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ⊢ φ
∀h φ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ ⊢ ∀h φ
t: tm Γ A
r: (∀h φ) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ⊢ φ
r':= hyperdoctrine_proof_subst ⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩ r: ((∀h φ) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))]) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]
⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]
∀h φ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ ⊢ ∀h φ
t: tm Γ A
r: (∀h φ) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ⊢ φ
r': (∀h φ)
[(π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩ ]tm]
⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]
∀h φ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ ⊢ ∀h φ
t: tm Γ A
r: (∀h φ) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ⊢ φ
r': (∀h φ) [tm_var Γ] ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]
∀h φ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ ⊢ ∀h φ
t: tm Γ A
r: (∀h φ) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ⊢ φ
r': ∀h φ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]
∀h φ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]

  exact r'.
Qed.

p: t · π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A)) = t' · s

hk
· ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
  π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩ = t **
hk · π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) = t'

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂, A: ty H
s: tm Γ₁ Γ₂
Γ': hyperdoctrine_type_category H
t: hyperdoctrine_type_category H ⟦ Γ', Γ₂ ×h A ⟧
t': hyperdoctrine_type_category H ⟦ Γ', Γ₁ ⟧
p: t · π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A)) = t' · s
isaprop
  {hk
  : hyperdoctrine_type_category H ⟦ Γ', Γ₁ ×h A ⟧ &
  hk
  · ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
    π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩ = t **
  hk · π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) = t'}
 abstract
      (use invproofirrelevance ;
       intros ζ₁ ζ₂ ;
       use subtypePath ; [ intro ; apply isapropdirprod ; apply homset_property | ] ;
       refine (hyperdoctrine_pair_eta _ @ _ @ !(hyperdoctrine_pair_eta _)) ;
       pose (pr22 ζ₁) as q ;
       rewrite hyperdoctrine_pr1_comp in q ;
       rewrite id_right in q ;
       rewrite q ; clear q ;
       pose (pr22 ζ₂) as q ;
       rewrite hyperdoctrine_pr1_comp in q ;
       rewrite id_right in q ;
       rewrite q ; clear q ;
       apply maponpaths ;
       pose (maponpaths (λ z, π₂ z) (pr12 ζ₁)) as q ; cbn in q ;
       rewrite (hyperdoctrine_pair_comp (H := H)) in q ;
       unfold tm_subst in q ;
       rewrite !assoc in q ;
       rewrite (hyperdoctrine_pr1_comp (H := H)) in q ;
       rewrite hyperdoctrine_pr2_comp in q ;
       rewrite !id_right in q ;
       rewrite hyperdoctrine_pair_pr2 in q ;
       rewrite q ;
       clear q ;
       pose (maponpaths (λ z, π₂ z) (pr12 ζ₂)) as q ; cbn in q ;
       rewrite (hyperdoctrine_pair_comp (H := H)) in q ;
       unfold tm_subst in q ;
       rewrite !assoc in q ;
       rewrite (hyperdoctrine_pr1_comp (H := H)) in q ;
       rewrite hyperdoctrine_pr2_comp in q ;
       rewrite !id_right in q ;
       rewrite hyperdoctrine_pair_pr2 in q ;
       rewrite q ;
       clear q ;
       apply idpath).

Γ₁, Γ₂, A: ty H
s: tm Γ₁ Γ₂
Γ': hyperdoctrine_type_category H

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂, A: ty H
s: tm Γ₁ Γ₂
Γ': hyperdoctrine_type_category H
t: hyperdoctrine_type_category H ⟦ Γ', Γ₂ ×h A ⟧
t': hyperdoctrine_type_category H ⟦ Γ', Γ₁ ⟧
p: t · π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A)) = t' · s
⟨ t', t · π₂ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A)) ⟩
· ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
  π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩ = t
 abstract
        (rewrite hyperdoctrine_pair_comp ;
         unfold tm_subst ;
         rewrite !assoc ;
         rewrite hyperdoctrine_pair_comp_pr1' ;
         rewrite hyperdoctrine_pair_comp_pr2' ;
         rewrite <- p ;
         rewrite hyperdoctrine_pr1_comp ;
         rewrite hyperdoctrine_pr2_comp ;
         rewrite !id_right ;
         rewrite <- hyperdoctrine_pair_eta ;
         apply idpath).
    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂, A: ty H
s: tm Γ₁ Γ₂
Γ': hyperdoctrine_type_category H

t': hyperdoctrine_type_category H ⟦ Γ', Γ₁ ⟧

⟨ t', t · π₂ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A)) ⟩
· π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) = t'
 abstract
        (rewrite hyperdoctrine_pair_comp_pr1' ;
         apply idpath).
Defined.

      ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
      π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩
    ∙ Core.right_adjoint
        ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₁ ×h A) Γ₁
           (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A))))) φ): z_iso
  ((Core.right_adjoint
      ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₂ ×h A) Γ₂
         (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A))))
    ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving (pr12 (pr1 H))
        (hyperdoctrine_cleaving (pr1 H)) s) φ)
  ((fiber_functor_from_cleaving (pr12 (pr1 H))
      (hyperdoctrine_cleaving (pr1 H))
      ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
      π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩
    ∙ Core.right_adjoint
        ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₁ ×h A) Γ₁
           (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A))))) φ)
∀h (φ
    [⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
     π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩]) ⊢ (∀h φ) [s]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂, A: ty H
s: tm Γ₁ Γ₂
φ: form (Γ₂ ×h A)
p:= (pr212 (pr222 (pr22 H))) Γ₂ (Γ₂ ×h A) Γ₁ (Γ₁ ×h A)
  (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A))) s (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)))
  ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
  π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩
  (! quantifier_subst_pb_eq A s)
  (quantifier_subst_pb A s) φ: is_z_isomorphism
  (right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans
     ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₂ ×h A) Γ₂
        (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A))))
     ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₁ ×h A) Γ₁
        (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A))))
     (comm_nat_z_iso_inv
        (hyperdoctrine_cleaving (pr1 H))
        (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A))) s
        (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)))
        ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
        π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩
        (! quantifier_subst_pb_eq A s)) φ)
f:= right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans
  ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₂ ×h A) Γ₂
     (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A))))
  ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₁ ×h A) Γ₁
     (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A))))
  (comm_nat_z_iso_inv
     (hyperdoctrine_cleaving (pr1 H))
     (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A))) s
     (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)))
     ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
     π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩
     (! quantifier_subst_pb_eq A s)) φ,, p
:
z_iso
  ((Core.right_adjoint
      ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₂ ×h A) Γ₂
         (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A))))
    ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving (pr12 (pr1 H))
        (hyperdoctrine_cleaving (pr1 H)) s) φ)
  ((fiber_functor_from_cleaving (pr12 (pr1 H))
      (hyperdoctrine_cleaving (pr1 H))
      ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
      π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩
    ∙ Core.right_adjoint
        ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₁ ×h A) Γ₁
           (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A))))) φ): z_iso
  ((Core.right_adjoint
      ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₂ ×h A) Γ₂
         (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A))))
    ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving (pr12 (pr1 H))
        (hyperdoctrine_cleaving (pr1 H)) s) φ)
  ((fiber_functor_from_cleaving (pr12 (pr1 H))
      (hyperdoctrine_cleaving (pr1 H))
      ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
      π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩
    ∙ Core.right_adjoint
        ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₁ ×h A) Γ₁
           (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A))))) φ)
(∀h φ) [s]
⊢ ∀h (φ
      [⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
       π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩])
 apply f.
  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂, A: ty H

φ: form (Γ₂ ×h A)
p:= (pr212 (pr222 (pr22 H))) Γ₂ (Γ₂ ×h A) Γ₁ (Γ₁ ×h A)

        π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩

f:= right_beck_chevalley_nat_trans
  ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₂ ×h A) Γ₂

  ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₁ ×h A) Γ₁
     (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A))))
  (comm_nat_z_iso_inv

     (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A))) s
     (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)))

      ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₂ ×h A) Γ₂

  ((fiber_functor_from_cleaving (pr12 (pr1 H))
      (hyperdoctrine_cleaving (pr1 H))
      ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
      π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩
    ∙ Core.right_adjoint
        ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₁ ×h A) Γ₁
           (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A))))) φ): z_iso
  ((Core.right_adjoint
      ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₂ ×h A) Γ₂
         (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A))))
    ∙ fiber_functor_from_cleaving (pr12 (pr1 H))

  ((fiber_functor_from_cleaving (pr12 (pr1 H))
      (hyperdoctrine_cleaving (pr1 H))
      ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,

    ∙ Core.right_adjoint
        ((pr112 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₁ ×h A) Γ₁
           (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A))))) φ)
∀h (φ
    [⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
     π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩]) ⊢ (∀h φ) [s]
 exact (inv_from_z_iso f).
Qed.

(** * 9. Existential quantification *)
Definition first_order_hyperdoctrine_exists
           {H : first_order_hyperdoctrine}
           {Γ A : ty H}
           (φ : form (Γ ×h A))
  : form Γ
  := dep_sum (pr2 (pr222 (pr222 H))) (π₁ (identity (Γ ×h A))) φ.

Notation "'∃h' φ" := (first_order_hyperdoctrine_exists φ) (at level 10)
    : hyperdoctrine.


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂, A: ty H
s: tm Γ₁ Γ₂
φ: form (Γ₂ ×h A)
(∃h φ) [s] =
∃h (φ
    [⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
     π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩])

        (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)))
        ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ]tm,
        π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩
        (! quantifier_subst_pb_eq A s)) φ)
f:= left_beck_chevalley_nat_trans
  ((pr122 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₂ ×h A) Γ₂
     (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A))))
  ((pr122 (pr222 (pr22 H))) (Γ₁ ×h A) Γ₁

     (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₂ ×h A))) s
     (π₁ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)))

     π₂ (tm_var (Γ₁ ×h A)) ⟩
     (! quantifier_subst_pb_eq A s)) φ,, p
:

  ((fiber_functor_from_cleaving (pr12 (pr1 H))
      (hyperdoctrine_cleaving (pr1 H))

  [⟨ (π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))) [tm_var (Γ ×h A) ]tm,
   (π₂ (tm_var ((Γ ×h A) ×h A)))
   [⟨ tm_var (Γ ×h A), π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ⟩ ]tm ⟩]

φ: form (Γ ×h A)
Δ: form Γ
φ ∧ Δ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))]
⊢ (Δ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ∧ φ)
  [⟨ (π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))) [tm_var (Γ ×h A) ]tm,
   π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ⟩]

  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)), π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ⟩]

  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)), π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ⟩]
  ∧ φ [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)), π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ⟩]

    apply hyperdoctrine_hyp.

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H

q: Δ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ∧ φ
⊢ ψ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))]
r: ∃h (ψ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))]) ⊢ ψ
∃h (Δ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ∧ φ)
⊢ ∃h (ψ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))])

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ, ψ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
p: Δ ⊢ ∃h φ
q: Δ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ∧ φ
⊢ ψ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))]
r: ∃h (ψ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))]) ⊢ ψ
(pr12 (pr1 H))[{Γ ×h A}]
⟦ Δ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ∧ φ,
ψ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))] ⟧

  exact q.
Qed.

(** * 10. Equality *)
Definition first_order_hyperdoctrine_equal
           {H : first_order_hyperdoctrine}
           {Γ A : ty H}
           (t₁ t₂ : tm Γ A)
  : form Γ
  := (dep_sum (pr2 (pr222 (pr222 H))) (Δ_{A}) ⊤) [ ⟨ t₁ , t₂ ⟩ ].

Notation "t₁ ≡ t₂" := (first_order_hyperdoctrine_equal t₁ t₂)
    : hyperdoctrine.


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂, A: ty H
s: hyperdoctrine_type_category H ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧
t₁, t₂: tm Γ₂ A
(t₁ ≡ t₂) [s] = (t₁ [s ]tm ≡ t₂ [s ]tm)


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂, A: ty H
s: hyperdoctrine_type_category H ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧
t₁, t₂: tm Γ₂ A
(t₁ ≡ t₂) [s] = (t₁ [s ]tm ≡ t₂ [s ]tm)

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂, A: ty H
s: hyperdoctrine_type_category H ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧
t₁, t₂: tm Γ₂ A
((dep_sum (pr222 (pr222 (pr2 H))) Δ_{ A} ⊤)
 [⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩]) [s] =
(dep_sum (pr222 (pr222 (pr2 H))) Δ_{ A} ⊤)
[⟨ t₁ [s ]tm, t₂ [s ]tm ⟩]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂, A: ty H
s: hyperdoctrine_type_category H ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧
t₁, t₂: tm Γ₂ A
(dep_sum (pr222 (pr222 (pr2 H))) Δ_{ A} ⊤)
[⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩ [s ]tm] =
(dep_sum (pr222 (pr222 (pr2 H))) Δ_{ A} ⊤)
[⟨ t₁ [s ]tm, t₂ [s ]tm ⟩]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ₁, Γ₂, A: ty H
s: hyperdoctrine_type_category H ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧
t₁, t₂: tm Γ₂ A
(dep_sum (pr222 (pr222 (pr2 H))) Δ_{ A} ⊤)
[⟨ t₁ [s ]tm, t₂ [s ]tm ⟩] =
(dep_sum (pr222 (pr222 (pr2 H))) Δ_{ A} ⊤)
[⟨ t₁ [s ]tm, t₂ [s ]tm ⟩]

  apply idpath.
Qed.

   π₂ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ⟩]

  [⟨ Δ_{ A} [π₁ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ]tm,
   π₂ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ⟩]

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
φ: form (Γ ×h A ×h A)
p: ⊤
⊢ φ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
   ⟨ π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)), π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ⟩
   ⟩]
t₁, t₂: tm Γ A
s:= hyperdoctrine_eq_elim_help_con_sub Γ A: tm ((A ×h A) ×h Γ) (Γ ×h A ×h A)
p':= hyperdoctrine_proof_subst
  ⟨ π₂ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)), π₁ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ⟩ p: ⊤
[⟨ π₂ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)), π₁ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ⟩]
⊢ (φ
   [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
    ⟨ π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)), π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))
    ⟩ ⟩])
  [⟨ π₂ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)), π₁ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ⟩]
⊤
⊢ φ
  [⟨ π₂ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)),
   ⟨ π₁ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)), π₁ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ⟩ ⟩]

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
φ: form (Γ ×h A ×h A)
p: ⊤
⊢ φ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
   ⟨ π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)), π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ⟩
   ⟩]
t₁, t₂: tm Γ A
s:= hyperdoctrine_eq_elim_help_con_sub Γ A: tm ((A ×h A) ×h Γ) (Γ ×h A ×h A)
p': ⊤
⊢ (φ
   [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
    ⟨ π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)), π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))
    ⟩ ⟩])
  [⟨ π₂ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)), π₁ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ⟩]
⊤
⊢ φ
  [⟨ π₂ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)),
   ⟨ π₁ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)), π₁ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ⟩ ⟩]

[⟨ π₂ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)), π₁ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ⟩]

  [⟨ π₂ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)),
   ⟨ π₁ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)), π₁ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ⟩ ⟩]

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
φ: form (Γ ×h A ×h A)
p: ⊤
⊢ φ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
   Δ_{ A} [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]
t₁, t₂: tm Γ A
s:= hyperdoctrine_eq_elim_help_con_sub Γ A: tm ((A ×h A) ×h Γ) (Γ ×h A ×h A)
q: ⊤
⊢ (φ [s])
  [⟨ Δ_{ A} [π₁ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ]tm,
   π₂ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ⟩]
t₁ ≡ t₂ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, ⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩ ⟩]

⊢ (φ [s])
  [⟨ Δ_{ A} [π₁ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ]tm,
   π₂ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ⟩]

 [⟨ π₂ (tm_var ((A ×h A) ×h Γ)),
  ⟨ (π₁ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
    [π₁ (tm_var ((A ×h A) ×h Γ)) ]tm,

   [⟨ ⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩, tm_var Γ ⟩ ]tm,
 ⟨ ((π₁ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
    [π₁ (tm_var ((A ×h A) ×h Γ)) ]tm)
   [⟨ ⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩, tm_var Γ ⟩ ]tm,

  ]tm) [⟨ ⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩, tm_var Γ ⟩ ]tm ⟩ ⟩]

  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
   Δ_{ A} [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]

 ⟨ (π₁ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
   [(π₁ (tm_var ((A ×h A) ×h Γ)))
    [⟨ ⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩, tm_var Γ ⟩ ]tm ]tm,
 (π₂ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
 [(π₁ (tm_var ((A ×h A) ×h Γ)))
  [⟨ ⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩, tm_var Γ ⟩ ]tm ]tm ⟩ ⟩]
⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, ⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩ ⟩]

q: ⊤
⊢ (φ [s])

   π₂ (tm_var (A ×h Γ)) ⟩]

 ⟨ t₁, (π₂ (tm_var (A ×h A))) [⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩ ]tm ⟩ ⟩]

  apply hyperdoctrine_hyp.

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
t₁, t₂: tm Γ A
p: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
q: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩]
Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine

Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
t₁, t₂: tm Γ A
p: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
q: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩]
Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
t₁, t₂: tm Γ A
p: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
q: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩]
ψ:= φ
[⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),
 (π₁ (tm_var (A ×h A))) [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A))
 ]tm ⟩]
⇒ φ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),
   (π₂ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
   [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]: form (Γ ×h A ×h A)
Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]

⊤
⊢ ψ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
   Δ_{ A} [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]

t₁, t₂: tm Γ A
p: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
q: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩]
ψ:= φ
[⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),
 (π₁ (tm_var (A ×h A))) [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A))
 ]tm ⟩]
⇒ φ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),
   (π₂ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
   [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]: form (Γ ×h A ×h A)
⊤
⊢ (φ
   [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),
    (π₁ (tm_var (A ×h A))) [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A))
    ]tm ⟩])
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
   Δ_{ A} [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]
  ⇒ (φ
     [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),
      (π₂ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
      [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)) ]tm ⟩])
    [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
     Δ_{ A} [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]

  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),

   ]tm ⟩
   [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),

φ: form (Γ ×h A)
t₁, t₂: tm Γ A
p: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
q: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩]
ψ:= φ
[⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),
 (π₁ (tm_var (A ×h A))) [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A))
 ]tm ⟩]
⇒ φ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),
   (π₂ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
   [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]: form (Γ ×h A ×h A)
r: ⊤
⊢ ψ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
   Δ_{ A} [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]
r': t₁ ≡ t₂
⊢ φ
  [⟨ (π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)))
     [⟨ tm_var Γ, ⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩ ⟩ ]tm,
   (π₁ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
   [(π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)))
    [⟨ tm_var Γ, ⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩ ⟩ ]tm ]tm ⟩]
  ⇒ φ
    [⟨ (π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)))
       [⟨ tm_var Γ, ⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩ ⟩ ]tm,
     (π₂ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
     [(π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)))
      [⟨ tm_var Γ, ⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩ ⟩ ]tm ]tm ⟩]
Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
t₁, t₂: tm Γ A
p: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
q: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩]
ψ:= φ
[⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),
 (π₁ (tm_var (A ×h A))) [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A))
 ]tm ⟩]
⇒ φ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),
   (π₂ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
   [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]: form (Γ ×h A ×h A)
r: ⊤
⊢ ψ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
   Δ_{ A} [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]
r': t₁ ≡ t₂
⊢ φ
  [⟨ tm_var Γ,
   (π₁ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
   [(π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)))
    [⟨ tm_var Γ, ⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩ ⟩ ]tm ]tm ⟩]
  ⇒ φ
    [⟨ tm_var Γ,
     (π₂ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
     [(π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)))
      [⟨ tm_var Γ, ⟨ t₁, t₂ ⟩ ⟩ ]tm ]tm ⟩]
Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine

φ: form (Γ ×h A)
t₁, t₂: tm Γ A

 (π₁ (tm_var (A ×h A))) [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A))
 ]tm ⟩]

r: ⊤
⊢ ψ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
   Δ_{ A} [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]
r': t₁ ≡ t₂
⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩] ⇒ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]
Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
t₁, t₂: tm Γ A
p: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
q: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩]
ψ:= φ
[⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),
 (π₁ (tm_var (A ×h A))) [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A))
 ]tm ⟩]
⇒ φ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),
   (π₂ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
   [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]: form (Γ ×h A ×h A)
r: ⊤
⊢ ψ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
   Δ_{ A} [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]
r': t₁ ≡ t₂
⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩] ⇒ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]
Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩] ⇒ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
φ: form (Γ ×h A)
t₁, t₂: tm Γ A
p: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
q: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩]
ψ:= φ
[⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),
 (π₁ (tm_var (A ×h A))) [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A))
 ]tm ⟩]
⇒ φ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)),
   (π₂ (tm_var (A ×h A)))
   [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]: form (Γ ×h A ×h A)
r: ⊤
⊢ ψ
  [⟨ π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
   Δ_{ A} [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm ⟩]
r': t₁ ≡ t₂
⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩] ⇒ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]
t₁ ≡ t₂ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩] ⇒ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]

  exact r'.
Qed.

  (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))
   ≡ t₁ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm) p q: Δ

  [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]

⊢ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩ ]tm
  ≡ (t₃ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩
    ]tm

p: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
p': Δ ⊢ t₂ ≡ t₃
φ:= π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ≡ t₃ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm
:
form (Γ ×h A): form (Γ ×h A)
Δ
⊢ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩ ]tm
  ≡ t₃ [(π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩ ]tm
    ]tm

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
t₁, t₂, t₃: tm Γ A
p: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
p': Δ ⊢ t₂ ≡ t₃
φ:= π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ≡ t₃ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm
:
form (Γ ×h A): form (Γ ×h A)
q: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]
r:= hyperdoctrine_eq_elim φ (hyperdoctrine_eq_sym p) q: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩]
Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₃

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine

r:= hyperdoctrine_eq_elim
  (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))
   ≡ t₃ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm)
  (hyperdoctrine_eq_sym p) q: Δ
⊢ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))
   ≡ t₃ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm)
  [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩]

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
t₁, t₂: tm Γ A
φ: form A
p: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
q: Δ ⊢ φ [t₁]
r: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂ ∧ φ [t₁]
h:= hyperdoctrine_eq_elim (φ [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))])
  (weaken_left (hyperdoctrine_hyp (t₁ ≡ t₂))
     ((φ [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))]) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩]))
  (weaken_right
     (hyperdoctrine_hyp
        ((φ [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))])
         [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩])) (t₁ ≡ t₂)): t₁ ≡ t₂
∧ (φ [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))]) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩]
⊢ (φ [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))]) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]
t₁ ≡ t₂ ∧ φ [t₁] ⊢ φ [t₂]

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A: ty H
Δ: form Γ
t₁, t₂: tm Γ A
φ: form A
p: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
q: Δ ⊢ φ [t₁]
r: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂ ∧ φ [t₁]
h: t₁ ≡ t₂
∧ φ [(π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩ ]tm]
⊢ φ [(π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩ ]tm]
t₁ ≡ t₂ ∧ φ [t₁] ⊢ φ [t₂]

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A, B: ty H
Δ: form Γ
t, t': tm Γ (A ×h B)
p: Δ ⊢ t ≡ t'
φ:= (π₁ t) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)) ]tm
≡ π₁ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)))
:
form (Γ ×h A ×h B): form (Γ ×h A ×h B)
Δ
⊢ π₁ t
  ≡ π₁
      (π₂
         ((tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩ ]tm))

    
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A, B: ty H
Δ: form Γ
t, t': tm Γ (A ×h B)
p: Δ ⊢ t ≡ t'
φ:= (π₁ t) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)) ]tm
≡ π₁ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)))
:
form (Γ ×h A ×h B): form (Γ ×h A ×h B)
Δ ⊢ π₁ t ≡ π₁ (π₂ ⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩)

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A, B: ty H

t, t': tm Γ (A ×h B)
p: Δ ⊢ t ≡ t'
φ:= (π₁ t) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)) ]tm
≡ π₁ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)))
:
form (Γ ×h A ×h B): form (Γ ×h A ×h B)
r: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]
r':= hyperdoctrine_eq_elim
  ((π₁ t) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)) ]tm
   ≡ π₁ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)))) p r: Δ
⊢ ((π₁ t) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)) ]tm
   ≡ π₁ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B))))
  [⟨ tm_var Γ, t' ⟩]

form (Γ ×h A ×h B): form (Γ ×h A ×h B)
r: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]
r': Δ
⊢ (π₂ t) [π₁ ⟨ tm_var Γ, t' ⟩ ]tm
  ≡ (π₂ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B))))
    [⟨ tm_var Γ, t' ⟩ ]tm
Δ ⊢ π₂ t ≡ π₂ t'

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A, B: ty H
Δ: form Γ
t, t': tm Γ (A ×h B)
p: Δ ⊢ t ≡ t'
φ:= (π₂ t) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)) ]tm
≡ π₂ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)))
:
form (Γ ×h A ×h B): form (Γ ×h A ×h B)
r: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]
r': Δ
⊢ (π₂ t) [tm_var Γ ]tm
  ≡ (π₂ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B))))
    [⟨ tm_var Γ, t' ⟩ ]tm
Δ ⊢ π₂ t ≡ π₂ t'

  ≡ (π₂ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B))))

Γ, A, B: ty H

t, t': tm Γ (A ×h B)

:

⊢ π₂ t
  ≡ π₂
      (π₂
         ((tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B))
          [⟨ tm_var Γ, t' ⟩ ]tm))

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A, B: ty H
Δ: form Γ
t, t': tm Γ (A ×h B)
p: Δ ⊢ t ≡ t'
φ:= (π₂ t) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)) ]tm
≡ π₂ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)))
:
form (Γ ×h A ×h B): form (Γ ×h A ×h B)
r: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]
r': Δ ⊢ π₂ t ≡ π₂ (π₂ ⟨ tm_var Γ, t' ⟩)
Δ ⊢ π₂ t ≡ π₂ t'

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A, B: ty H
Δ: form Γ
t, t': tm Γ (A ×h B)
p: Δ ⊢ t ≡ t'
φ:= (π₂ t) [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)) ]tm
≡ π₂ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A ×h B)))
:
form (Γ ×h A ×h B): form (Γ ×h A ×h B)
r: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t ⟩]
r': Δ ⊢ π₂ t ≡ π₂ t'
Δ ⊢ π₂ t ≡ π₂ t'

  exact r'.
Qed.

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A, B: ty H
Δ: form Γ
s₁, s₂: tm Γ A
p: Δ ⊢ s₁ ≡ s₂
t: tm Γ B
φ:= ⟨ s₁ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm,

≡ ⟨ π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
  t [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm ⟩
:
form (Γ ×h A): form (Γ ×h A)
r: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₁ ⟩]
r':= hyperdoctrine_eq_elim φ p r: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩]
Δ ⊢ ⟨ s₁, t ⟩ ≡ ⟨ s₂, t ⟩

r': Δ
⊢ ⟨ s₁
    [π₁ ((tm_var (Γ ×h A)) [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩ ]tm)
    ]tm,
  t [π₁ ((tm_var (Γ ×h A)) [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩ ]tm)
  ]tm ⟩
  ≡ ⟨ (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A))) [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩
      ]tm,
    t
    [π₁ ((tm_var (Γ ×h A)) [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩ ]tm)
    ]tm ⟩
Δ ⊢ ⟨ s₁, t ⟩ ≡ ⟨ s₂, t ⟩

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A, B: ty H
Δ: form Γ
s₁, s₂: tm Γ A
p: Δ ⊢ s₁ ≡ s₂
t: tm Γ B
φ:= ⟨ s₁ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm,
t [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm ⟩
≡ ⟨ π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)),
  t [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h A)) ]tm ⟩
:
form (Γ ×h A): form (Γ ×h A)
r: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₁ ⟩]
r': Δ
⊢ ⟨ s₁
    [π₁ ((tm_var (Γ ×h A)) [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩ ]tm)
    ]tm,
  t [π₁ ((tm_var (Γ ×h A)) [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩ ]tm)
  ]tm ⟩
  ≡ ⟨ π₂
        ((tm_var (Γ ×h A)) [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩ ]tm),
    t
    [π₁ ((tm_var (Γ ×h A)) [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩ ]tm)
    ]tm ⟩
Δ ⊢ ⟨ s₁, t ⟩ ≡ ⟨ s₂, t ⟩

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A, B: ty H
Δ: form Γ
s: tm Γ A
t₁, t₂: tm Γ B
p: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
φ:= ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h B)) ]tm,

  π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h B)) ⟩
:
form (Γ ×h B): form (Γ ×h B)
r: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩]
r':= hyperdoctrine_eq_elim φ p r: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]
Δ ⊢ ⟨ s, t₁ ⟩ ≡ ⟨ s, t₂ ⟩

   ≡ ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h B)) ]tm,

⊢ (⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h B)) ]tm,
   t₁ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h B)) ]tm ⟩
   ≡ ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h B)) ]tm,
     π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h B)) ⟩) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩]

    ⟩

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine

s: tm Γ A
t₁, t₂: tm Γ B
p: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
φ:= ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h B)) ]tm,
t₁ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h B)) ]tm ⟩
≡ ⟨ s [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h B)) ]tm,
  π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h B)) ⟩
:
form (Γ ×h B): form (Γ ×h B)
r: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₁ ⟩]
r': Δ
⊢ ⟨ s
    [(π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h B))) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩ ]tm
    ]tm,
  t₁
  [(π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h B))) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩ ]tm
  ]tm ⟩
  ≡ ⟨ s
      [(π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h B))) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩
       ]tm ]tm,
    (π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h B))) [⟨ tm_var Γ, t₂ ⟩ ]tm
    ⟩
Δ ⊢ ⟨ s, t₁ ⟩ ≡ ⟨ s, t₂ ⟩

  exact r'.
Qed.


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A, B: ty H
Δ: form Γ
s₁, s₂: tm Γ A
p: Δ ⊢ s₁ ≡ s₂
t₁, t₂: tm Γ B
q: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
Δ ⊢ ⟨ s₁, t₁ ⟩ ≡ ⟨ s₂, t₂ ⟩


H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, A, B: ty H
Δ: form Γ
s₁, s₂: tm Γ A
p: Δ ⊢ s₁ ≡ s₂
t₁, t₂: tm Γ B
q: Δ ⊢ t₁ ≡ t₂
Δ ⊢ ⟨ s₁, t₁ ⟩ ≡ ⟨ s₂, t₂ ⟩

  exact (hyperdoctrine_eq_trans
           (hyperdoctrine_eq_pair_left p _)
           (hyperdoctrine_eq_pair_right _ q)).
Qed.

H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, Γ', B: ty H
Δ: form Γ
s₁, s₂: tm Γ Γ'

q: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₁ ⟩]
r:= hyperdoctrine_eq_elim φ p q: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩]
Δ ⊢ t [s₁ ]tm ≡ t [s₂ ]tm

⊢ t
  [s₁
   [π₁ ((tm_var (Γ ×h Γ')) [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩ ]tm)
   ]tm ]tm
  ≡ t
    [(π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h Γ'))) [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩ ]tm
    ]tm
Δ ⊢ t [s₁ ]tm ≡ t [s₂ ]tm

  
H: first_order_hyperdoctrine
Γ, Γ', B: ty H
Δ: form Γ
s₁, s₂: tm Γ Γ'
p: Δ ⊢ s₁ ≡ s₂
t: tm Γ' B
φ:= t [s₁ [π₁ (tm_var (Γ ×h Γ')) ]tm ]tm
≡ t [π₂ (tm_var (Γ ×h Γ')) ]tm: form (Γ ×h Γ')
q: Δ ⊢ φ [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₁ ⟩]
r: Δ
⊢ t
  [s₁
   [π₁ ((tm_var (Γ ×h Γ')) [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩ ]tm)
   ]tm ]tm
  ≡ t
    [π₂ ((tm_var (Γ ×h Γ')) [⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩ ]tm)
    ]tm
Δ ⊢ t [s₁ ]tm ≡ t [s₂ ]tm

⊢ t [s₁ [π₁ ⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩ ]tm ]tm
  ≡ t [π₂ ⟨ tm_var Γ, s₂ ⟩ ]tm
Δ ⊢ t [s₁ ]tm ≡ t [s₂ ]tm

(** * 12. Derived connectives *)

(** * 12.1. Bi-implication *)
Definition first_order_hyperdoctrine_iff
           {H : first_order_hyperdoctrine}
           {Γ : ty H}
           (φ ψ : form Γ)
  : form Γ
  := (φ ⇒ ψ) ∧ (ψ ⇒ φ).

Notation "φ ⇔ ψ" := (first_order_hyperdoctrine_iff φ ψ).

(** * 12.2. Negation *)
Definition first_order_hyperdoctrine_neg
           {H : first_order_hyperdoctrine}
           {Γ : ty H}
           (φ : form Γ)
  : form Γ
  := φ ⇒ ⊥.

(** * 13. A tactic for simplifying goals in the internal language of first-order hyperdoctrines *)

(**
  The tactic `hypersimplify` helps proving statements in the internal language of a hyperdoctrine.
  Such goals are of the shape `Δ ⊢ φ`. The tactic simplifies `Δ` and φ` by propagating the
  substitutions and by putting all terms that occur in either `Δ` or φ` in normal form. The tactic
  can print the rewrite statements that can replace it, by invoking `hypersimplify true` in Ltac2 or
  `hypersimplifyp` in Ltac1 (see the `Notation` commands further down).

  The tactic uses identities with two different levels:
  - The rewrites with level 0 are those that express how substitution acts on formulas, and are used
    to propagate substitutions in `Δ` and `φ`.
  - The rewrites with level 1 are all rewrite rules on terms in the language, used to normalize all
    terms in `Δ` and `φ`.

  In some cases, it is a bit faster to use `hypersimplify_form` to simplify the formula and delay using
  the full `hypersimplify` until it is necessary. The reason why this helps, is because one might
  have made the goal smaller and removed some unnecessary assumptions using weakening.
  This is demonstrated in `PERs.v` in the proof of [eq_per_axioms].

  The tactic can be extended with new traversals and rewrites. For example, handling of `~` is added
  in `PERs.v`.
 *)

Set Default Proof Mode "Ltac2".

Ltac2 mutable hypertraversals () : t_traversal list := [].

Ltac2 Set hypertraversals as traversals := fun _ =>
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (_  [ ?b]tm) = _ ] => '(λ x,  x [$b ]tm) end)  "" " [ _ ]tm") ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (?a [  _]tm) = _ ] => '(λ x,  $a[ x ]tm) end)    "_ [" "]tm") ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (_  [ ?b]  ) = _ ] => '(λ x,  x [$b ]  ) end) " " " [ _ ]"  ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (?a [  _]  ) = _ ] => '(λ x,  $a[ x ]  ) end)    "_ [" "]"  ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (_  ∧ ?b   ) = _ ] => '(λ x,  x ∧$b    ) end)  "" " ∧ _"    ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (?a ∧  _   ) = _ ] => '(λ x,  $a∧ x    ) end)    "_ ∧ " ""  ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (_  ∨ ?b   ) = _ ] => '(λ x,  x ∨$b    ) end)  "" " ∨ _"    ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (?a ∨  _   ) = _ ] => '(λ x,  $a∨ x    ) end)    "_ ∨ " ""  ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (_  ⇒ ?b   ) = _ ] => '(λ x,  x ⇒$b    ) end)  "" " ⇒ _"    ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (?a ⇒  _   ) = _ ] => '(λ x,  $a⇒ x    ) end)    "_ ⇒ " ""  ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (_  ≡ ?b   ) = _ ] => '(λ x,  x ≡$b    ) end)  "" " ≡ _"    ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (?a ≡  _   ) = _ ] => '(λ x,  $a≡ x    ) end)    "_ ≡ " ""  ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (_  ⇔ ?b   ) = _ ] => '(λ x,  x ⇔$b    ) end)  "" " ⇔ _"    ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (?a ⇔  _   ) = _ ] => '(λ x,  $a⇔ x    ) end)    "_ ⇔ " ""  ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (⟨_ ,?b⟩   ) = _ ] => '(λ x, ⟨x ,$b⟩   ) end) "⟨" " , _⟩"   ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (⟨?a, _⟩   ) = _ ] => '(λ x, ⟨$a, x⟩   ) end)   "⟨_ , " "⟩" ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (∀h _      ) = _ ] => '(λ x, ∀h x      ) end)  "∀h " ""     ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (∃h _      ) = _ ] => '(λ x, ∃h x      ) end)  "∃h " ""     ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (¬  _      ) = _ ] => '(λ x, ¬  x      ) end)   "¬ " ""     ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (π₁ _      ) = _ ] => '(λ x, π₁ x      ) end)  "π₁ " ""     ) ::
  (make_traversal (fun () => match! goal with | [|- (π₂ _      ) = _ ] => '(λ x, π₂ x      ) end)  "π₂ " ""     ) ::
  traversals ().

Ltac2 mutable hyperrewrites () : (int * t_rewrite) list := [].

Ltac2 Set hyperrewrites as rewrites := fun () =>
  (0, (pn:(⊤[_]),            (fun () => '(truth_subst _                 )), "truth_subst _"                 )) ::
  (0, (pn:(⊥[_]),            (fun () => '(false_subst _                 )), "false_subst _"                 )) ::
  (0, (pn:((_ ∧ _)[_]),      (fun () => '(conj_subst _ _ _              )), "conj_subst _ _ _"              )) ::
  (0, (pn:((_ ∨ _)[_]),      (fun () => '(disj_subst _ _ _              )), "disj_subst _ _ _"              )) ::
  (0, (pn:((_ ⇒ _)[_]),      (fun () => '(impl_subst _ _ _              )), "impl_subst _ _ _"              )) ::
  (0, (pn:((_ ⇔ _)[_]),      (fun () => '(iff_subst _ _ _               )), "iff_subst _ _ _"               )) ::
  (0, (pn:((_ ≡ _)[_]),      (fun () => '(equal_subst _ _ _             )), "equal_subst _ _ _"             )) ::
  (0, (pn:((∀h _)[_]),       (fun () => '(forall_subst _ _              )), "forall_subst _ _"              )) ::
  (0, (pn:((∃h _)[_]),       (fun () => '(exists_subst _ _              )), "exists_subst _ _"              )) ::
  (0, (pn:((¬ _)[_]),        (fun () => '(neg_subst _ _                 )), "neg_subst _ _"                 )) ::
  (0, (pn:((_[_])[_]),       (fun () => '(hyperdoctrine_comp_subst _ _ _)), "hyperdoctrine_comp_subst _ _ _")) ::
  (0, (pn:(_[tm_var _]),     (fun () => '(hyperdoctrine_id_subst _      )), "hyperdoctrine_id_subst _"      )) ::
  (1, (pn:((π₁ _)[_]tm),     (fun () => '(hyperdoctrine_pr1_subst _ _   )), "hyperdoctrine_pr1_subst _ _"   )) ::
  (1, (pn:((π₂ _)[_]tm),     (fun () => '(hyperdoctrine_pr2_subst _ _   )), "hyperdoctrine_pr2_subst _ _"   )) ::
  (1, (pn:(⟨_, _⟩[_]tm),     (fun () => '(hyperdoctrine_pair_subst _ _ _)), "hyperdoctrine_pair_subst _ _ _")) ::
  (1, (pn:((tm_var _)[_]tm), (fun () => '(var_tm_subst _                )), "var_tm_subst _"                )) ::
  (1, (pn:((_ [_]tm)[_]tm),  (fun () => '(tm_subst_comp _ _ _           )), "tm_subst_comp _ _ _"           )) ::
  (1, (pn:(_[tm_var _]tm),   (fun () => '(tm_subst_var _                )), "tm_subst_var _"                )) ::
  (1, (pn:(π₁⟨_, _⟩),        (fun () => '(hyperdoctrine_pair_pr1 _ _    )), "hyperdoctrine_pair_pr1 _ _"    )) ::
  (1, (pn:(π₂⟨_, _⟩),        (fun () => '(hyperdoctrine_pair_pr2 _ _    )), "hyperdoctrine_pair_pr2 _ _"    )) ::
  (1, (pn:(!![_]tm),         (fun () => '(hyperdoctrine_unit_tm_subst _ )), "hyperdoctrine_unit_tm_subst _ ")) ::
  rewrites ().

Ltac2 hypertop_traversals (ltac2 : bool) (print: bool) : ((unit -> unit) * navigation) list :=
  ((fun () => match! goal with
    | [ |- _ = _ ] => refine '(!(_ @ !_))
    end), {
      left := [""];
      right := [""];
      preinpostfix := (String.concat "" ["refine "; (if ltac2 then "'" else ""); "(_ @ !maponpaths "], " ", ").");
      print := print
  }) :: ((fun () => match! goal with
    | [ |- _ = _ ] => refine '(_ @ _)
    end), {
      left := [""];
      right := [""];
      preinpostfix := (String.concat "" ["refine "; (if ltac2 then "'" else ""); "(maponpaths "], " ", " @ _).");
      print := print
  }) :: ((fun () => match! goal with
    | [ |- ?a ⊢ _ ] => refine '(transportb (λ x, $a ⊢ x) _ _); cbv beta
    end), {
      left := ["_ ⊢ "];
      right := [""];
      preinpostfix := (String.concat "" ["refine "; (if ltac2 then "'" else ""); "(transportb "], " ", " _).");
      print := print
  }) :: ((fun () => match! goal with
    | [ |- _ ⊢ ?b ] => refine '(transportb (λ x, x ⊢ $b) _ _); cbv beta
    end), {
      left := [""];
      right := [" ⊢ _"];
      preinpostfix := (String.concat "" ["refine "; (if ltac2 then "'" else ""); "(transportb "], " ", " _).");
      print := print
  }) :: [].

Ltac2 hypersimplify0 (ltac2 : bool option) (print: bool option) : int option -> unit :=
  simplify
  (List.rev (hypertraversals ()))
  (List.rev (hyperrewrites ()))
  (List.rev (hypertop_traversals (Option.default true ltac2) (Option.default false print))).

Ltac2 Notation "hypersimplify" print(opt(next)) n(opt(next)) := hypersimplify0 (Some true) print (n).

Set Default Proof Mode "Classic".

Tactic Notation "hypersimplify" := ltac2:(hypersimplify0 (Some false) (Some false) None).
Tactic Notation "hypersimplifyp" := ltac2:(hypersimplify0 (Some false) (Some true) None).
Tactic Notation "hypersimplify_form" := ltac2:(hypersimplify0 (Some false) (Some false) (Some 0)).
Tactic Notation "hypersimplifyp_form" := ltac2:(hypersimplify0 (Some false) (Some true) (Some 0)).

Ltac simplify_form_step :=
  rewrite ?truth_subst,
    ?false_subst,
    ?conj_subst,
    ?disj_subst,
    ?impl_subst,
    ?forall_subst,
    ?exists_subst,
    ?equal_subst,
    ?iff_subst,
    ?neg_subst,
    ?hyperdoctrine_comp_subst,
    ?hyperdoctrine_id_subst.

Ltac simplify_form :=
  repeat (progress simplify_form_step).

Ltac simplify_term_step :=
  rewrite ?hyperdoctrine_pr1_subst,
    ?hyperdoctrine_pr2_subst,
    ?hyperdoctrine_pair_subst,
    ?var_tm_subst,
    ?tm_subst_comp,
    ?tm_subst_var,
    ?hyperdoctrine_pair_pr1,
    ?hyperdoctrine_pair_pr2,
    ?hyperdoctrine_unit_tm_subst.

Ltac simplify_term :=
  repeat (progress simplify_term_step).

Ltac simplify := simplify_form ; simplify_term.
